File: supabase/functions/generate-embeddings/index.ts
================================================
// supabase/functions/generate-embedding/index.ts
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std@0.192.0/http/server.ts';
import { supabase } from '../_shared/supabaseClient';

console.log('INFO: "generate-embedding" function initialized.');

/**
 * This function provides a dedicated endpoint to generate vector embeddings.
 * It acts as a proxy to the pg_vectorize 'embed' remote procedure call (RPC)
 * in the Supabase database, ensuring consistent model usage and security.
 *
 * Prerequisite: `vector` and `vectorize` extensions enabled in Supabase,
 * and `vectorize.init()` has been run.
 */
serve(async (req: Request) => {
  // Handle CORS preflight requests
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response('ok', {
      headers: {
        'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'POST, OPTIONS',
        'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, Authorization',
      },
    });
  }

  try {
    if (req.method !== 'POST') {
      throw new Error(`Method ${req.method} not allowed. Please use POST.`);
    }

    const { text } = await req.json();

    if (!text || typeof text !== 'string' || text.trim() === '') {
      throw new Error('Request body must contain a non-empty "text" property of type string.');
    }

    console.log(`INFO: Generating embedding for text starting with: "${text.substring(0, 50)}..."`);

    // Call the database function to generate the embedding.
    const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('embed', {
      content: text,
    });

    if (error) {
      console.error('Embedding RPC Error:', error);
      throw new Error(`Failed to generate embedding: ${error.message}`);
    }

    console.log('INFO: Embedding generated successfully.');

    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ embedding: data }),
      {
        status: 200,
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
      }
    );
  } catch (e: unknown) {
    const errorMessage = e instanceof Error ? e.message : 'An unknown error occurred.';
    console.error('CRITICAL ERROR in generate-embedding:', errorMessage);
    return new Response(
      JSON.stringify({ error: errorMessage }),
      {
        status: 400, // Client-side errors (bad request)
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json',
          'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
        },
      }
    );
  }
});

================================================
// supabase/functions/scrape-recipe/index.ts
import { serve } from 'https://deno.land/std@0.192.0/http/server.ts';

// FIX: Change these imports from '@shared/...' to direct relative paths.
import { fetchAndProcessRecipe } from '../_shared/core/processor.js';
import { DatabaseService } from '../_shared/services/databaseService.js';
import type { FetchProcessOptions } from '../_shared/types.js';

interface ScrapeRequestPayload {
  url: string;
  recipeIdOverride?: string | null;
  includeNutrition?: boolean;
  includeGemmaEnrichment?: boolean;
  generateRecipeEmbedding?: boolean;
}

serve(async (req) => {
  // 1. Handle CORS preflight requests
  if (req.method === 'OPTIONS') {
    return new Response('ok', {
      headers: { 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*', 'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'content-type, authorization' },
    });
  }

  try {
    // 2. Validate request method and body
    if (req.method !== 'POST') {
      throw new Error('Method Not Allowed. Please use POST.');
    }
    const payload: ScrapeRequestPayload = await req.json();
    const { url } = payload;

    if (!url || typeof url !== 'string') {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'URL is a required parameter and must be a string.' }), { status: 400 });
    }
    
    // 3. Basic URL syntax validation
    try {
      new URL(url);
    } catch (_) {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Invalid URL format provided.' }), { status: 400 });
    }

    console.log(`INFO (scrape-recipe): Received request for URL: ${url}`);
    const processOptions: FetchProcessOptions = {
      recipeIdOverride: payload.recipeIdOverride,
      includeNutrition: payload.includeNutrition ?? false,
      includeGemmaEnrichment: payload.includeGemmaEnrichment ?? false,
      generateRecipeEmbeddingFlag: payload.generateRecipeEmbedding ?? false,
    };

    // 4. Call the core processing logic
    const processedRecipe = await fetchAndProcessRecipe(url, processOptions);
    if (!processedRecipe) {
      return new Response(
        JSON.stringify({ error: 'Recipe could not be processed. The URL may not contain a valid recipe or the site is unsupported.' }),
        { status: 404, headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' } }
      );
    }
    
    // 5. Save to the database
    const { data: savedData, error: dbError } = await DatabaseService.saveRecipe(processedRecipe);
    if (dbError) {
      // Re-throw to be caught by the main error handler, ensuring consistent error responses
      throw new Error(`Database save failed: ${dbError.message}`);
    }

    // 6. Return success response
    return new Response(JSON.stringify(savedData), {
      status: 200,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
    });

  } catch (e: unknown) {
    // 7. Centralized error handling
    const error = e instanceof Error ? e : new Error(String(e));
    console.error('CRITICAL (scrape-recipe): Top-level error caught:', error.message);
    
    // Determine appropriate status code
    const status = error.message.includes('Method Not Allowed') ? 405 : 500;

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: error.message }), {
      status,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*' },
    });
  }
});

File: test/imageUpload.test.ts

// Simple test script for Supabase image upload
import { downloadImage, uploadImageToSupabase } from '../src/utils/networkUtils.js';
import { initializeSupabase } from '../src/config/index.js';
import { config } from 'dotenv';
import { join } from 'path';

// Load environment variables from .env file
config({ path: join(process.cwd(), '.env') });

// Test image URL - using a small test image
const TEST_IMAGE_URL = 'https://picsum.photos/200/300';

async function testImageUpload() {
  // Check for required environment variables
  const supabaseUrl = process.env['SUPABASE_URL'];
  const supabaseKey = process.env['SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY'];
  
  if (!supabaseUrl || !supabaseKey) {
    console.warn('Skipping Supabase upload test - Missing Supabase credentials');
    console.log('Please set SUPABASE_URL and SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY in your .env file');
    return;
  }
  
  // Initialize Supabase with the environment variables
  console.log('Initializing Supabase client...');
  console.log('Supabase URL:', supabaseUrl);
  console.log('Supabase Key:', supabaseKey ? '*** (key provided)' : 'MISSING');
  
  try {
    const supabase = initializeSupabase(supabaseUrl, supabaseKey);
    console.log('Supabase client initialized successfully');
    
    // Verify storage is available
    if (!supabase.storage) {
      throw new Error('Supabase storage is not available. Check your Supabase configuration.');
    }
    
    // List buckets to verify storage access
    console.log('Listing storage buckets...');
    const { data: buckets, error: bucketsError } = await supabase.storage.listBuckets();
    
    if (bucketsError) {
      console.error('Error listing buckets:', bucketsError);
      return;
    }
    
    console.log('Available buckets:', buckets?.map(b => b.name).join(', ') || 'None');
    
    // Check if recipe_images bucket exists
    const recipeImagesBucket = buckets?.find(b => b.name === 'recipe_images');
    if (!recipeImagesBucket) {
      console.warn('WARNING: recipe_images bucket not found. It will be created on first upload if permissions allow.');
    }

    console.log('1. Downloading test image...');
    const imageBuffer = await downloadImage(TEST_IMAGE_URL);
    
    if (!imageBuffer) {
      console.error('Failed to download test image');
      return;
    }

    console.log('2. Image downloaded successfully, size:', imageBuffer.length, 'bytes');
    
    const recipeId = 'test-recipe-' + Date.now();
    console.log('3. Uploading to Supabase Storage with recipe ID:', recipeId);
    
    const imageUrl = await uploadImageToSupabase(
      imageBuffer,
      recipeId,
      TEST_IMAGE_URL,
      supabase // Pass the initialized Supabase client
    );

    if (imageUrl) {
      console.log('✅ Upload successful!');
      console.log('   Image URL:', imageUrl);
    } else {
      console.error('❌ Upload failed - check logs for details');
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Error during test:', error);
    if (error instanceof Error) {
      console.error('Error details:', {
        name: error.name,
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack?.split('\n').slice(0, 3).join('\n') + '...'
      });
    }
  }
}

// Run the test
console.log('Starting Supabase image upload test...');
testImageUpload()
  .then(() => console.log('Test completed'))
  .catch(err => console.error('Test failed:', err));
